[30;1m239 | [0m[35m- Switched to a new streaming approach when writing files, keeping memory-usage at a minimum:[0m
[30;1m240 | [0m[35m  - Specify filepath/destination and text encoding when creating the Writer. [0m
[30;1m241 | [0m[35m  - The file is written incrementally with each call to shape/record. [0m
[30;1m242 | [0m[35m  - Adding shapes is now done using dedicated methods for each shapetype. [0m

[30;1m567 | [0m[35m  * Field length: the length of the data found at this column index. Older GIS[0m
[30;1m568 | [0m[35m	   software may truncate this length to 8 or 11 characters for "Character"[0m
[30;1m569 | [0m[35m	   fields.[0m
[30;1m570 | [0m[35m  * Decimal length: the number of decimal places found in "Number" fields.[0m
